                FEMA Telephone Directory (FTD) as of November 1992

Telephone numbers marked with an asterisk (*) are Secure Telephone Units.
For FTS 2000 and commercial long distance calls, dial 9+1+10-digit phone number.
For FEMA Switched Network (FSN) calls, dial 6+FSN exchange+4-digit extension.

To find an entry type the letter 'F' followed by the text you want to find.
Press the 'Enter' key to begin the search.  Type the letter 'A' to find the
next occurrence of the same text.

                FEMA Telephone Directory (FTD) as of November 1992

Telephone numbers marked with an asterisk (*) are Secure Telephone Units.
For FTS 2000 and commercial long distance calls, dial 9+1+10-digit phone number.
For FEMA Switched Network (FSN) calls, dial 6+FSN exchange+4-digit extension.

To find an entry type the letter 'F' followed by the text you want to find.
Press the 'Enter' key to begin the search.  Type the letter 'A' to find the
next occurrence of the same text.

                FEMA Telephone Directory (FTD) as of November 1992

Telephone numbers marked with an asterisk (*) are Secure Telephone Units.
For FTS 2000 and commercial long distance calls, dial 9+1+10-digit phone number.
For FEMA Switched Network (FSN) calls, dial 6+FSN exchange+4-digit extension.

To find an entry type the letter 'F' followed by the text you want to find.
Press the 'Enter' key to begin the search.  Type the letter 'A' to find the
next occurrence of the same text.

                FEMA Telephone Directory (FTD) as of November 1992

Telephone numbers marked with an asterisk (*) are Secure Telephone Units.
For FTS 2000 and commercial long distance calls, dial 9+1+10-digit phone number.
For FEMA Switched Network (FSN) calls, dial 6+FSN exchange+4-digit extension.

To find an entry type the letter 'F' followed by the text you want to find.
Press the 'Enter' key to begin the search.  Type the letter 'A' to find the
next occurrence of the same text.
